        function loadScriptFile(file,id,skipIfExist,callbackLaodCompleted) {
            // Get the first script element on the page
            var refs = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );

            if(!refs)
                return;

            var alreadyAdded = false;

            if(id)
                for(var i = 0 ; i < refs.length ; i++){
                    var ccRef = refs[i];
                    if(ccRef && ccRef.src === file){
                        if(skipIfExist === true){
                            alreadyAdded = true;
                            break;
                        }

                        var elem = document.getElementById(id)
                        if(elem)
                            elem.parentNode.removeChild(elem)
                    }
                }

            if(alreadyAdded && skipIfExist){
                if(callbackLaodCompleted){
                    callbackLaodCompleted();
                }
                return;
            }


            var script = document.createElement( 'script' );
            script.src = file+ '?v=1.02.416.52047d5';
            if(id)
                script.id = id;

            refs[0].parentNode.insertBefore( script, refs[0] );
            if(callbackLaodCompleted){
                script.onload = function () {
                    callbackLaodCompleted();
                }
            }
        }

        var io_bbout_element_id = 'device_fingerprint'; //the input id will be used to collect the device fingerprint value

        var io_exclude_stm = 0;//prevent the iovation Active X control from running on either Windows
        var io_install_flash = false;
        var io_enable_rip = true;// collect real ip information

    </script>

<script id="dmd-sdk-stub-script" src="https://sdk-cdn.mazeedplus.com/stub.js" type="text/javascript"></script><script type="text/javascript" async="" src="https://sdk-cdn.mazeedplus.com/sdk.js" crossorigin="anonymous" id="dmd-sdk-script"></script>

<script>
// User identification for dmdSdk
(function() {
    var retryCount = 0;
    var maxRetries = 5;

    function identifyUser(customer) {
        try {
            if (!customer) {
                return;
            }

            if (window.dmdSdk) {
                const userIdentities = {};

                if (customer.id) {
                    userIdentities.userId = customer.id;
                }
                if (customer.email) {
                    userIdentities.email = customer.email;
                }
                if (customer.mobile) {
                    userIdentities.mobile = customer.mobile;
                }

                window.dmdSdk.Identity.identify({
                    userIdentities
                });
            } else {
                retryCount++;
                if (retryCount <= maxRetries) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        identifyUser(customer);
                    }, 100);
                } else {
                    console.warn('dmdSdk not available after ' + maxRetries + ' retries. User identification skipped.');
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('User identification error:', error);
        }
    }

    // Priority 1: Use session customer data (for lazy-load stores)
    if (window.ZidIdentifyMomentCustomer) {
        identifyUser(window.ZidIdentifyMomentCustomer);
    }
    // Priority 2: Use window.customer (already loaded)
    else if (window.customer) {
        identifyUser(window.customer);
    }
    // Priority 3: Wait for customerAsync (lazy loading)
    else if (window.customerAsync) {
        window.customerAsync.then(function(customer) {
            identifyUser(customer);
        }).catch(function(error) {
            console.error('Error loading customer:', error);
        });
    }
})();
</script>
